  <span m="885850">radicals,</span> <span m="886360">which</span> <span m="886510">are</span>
  <span m="886680">antioxidants.</span> <span m="887320">So</span> <span m="888240">you</span>
  <span m="888390">hear</span> <span m="888680">in</span> <span m="888770">a</span>
  <span m="888840">lot</span> <span m="889040">of</span> <span m="889520">different</span>
  <span m="889920">creams</span> <span m="890430">or</span> <span m="890870">products</span>
  <span m="891450">or</span> <span m="891590">vitamins</span> <span m="892120">that</span>
  <span m="892260">they</span> <span m="892390">have</span> <span m="892680">antioxidants</span>
  <span m="893440">in</span> <span m="893780">them,</span> <span m="893930">which</span>
  <span m="894120">get</span> <span m="894390">rid</span> <span m="894560">of</span>
  <span m="894670">free</span> <span m="894880">radicals.</span> <span m="895840">The</span>
  <span m="895960">reason</span> <span m="896290">you</span> <span m="896360">would</span>
  <span m="896490">want</span> <span m="896660">to</span> <span m="896720">get</span>
  <span m="896950">rid</span> <span m="897130">of</span> <span m="897230">free</span>
  <span m="897420">radicals</span> <span m="897910">is</span> <span m="898010">that</span>
  <span m="898200">free</span> <span m="898400">radicals</span> <span m="898900">can</span>
  <span m="899090">damage</span> <span m="899480">DNA,</span> <span m="900380">so</span>

  <span m="2973520">in</span> <span m="2973600">what</span> <span m="2973780">the</span>

  <span m="2975250">so</span> <span m="2975450">we</span> <span m="2975560">tend</span>
  <span m="2975860">to</span> <span m="2975960">pay</span> <span m="2976160">attention</span>
  <span m="2976570">to</span> <span m="2976670">them</span> <span m="2976900">in</span>
  <span m="2977000">terms</span> <span m="2977290">of</span> <span m="2977380">arrows.</span>
  <span m="2977900">Oh,</span> <span m="2978120">the</span> <span m="2978250">electrons</span>
  <span m="2978880">are</span> <span m="2978990">going</span> <span m="2979390">over</span>
  <span m="2979660">to</span> <span m="2979750">the</span> <span m="2979830">chlorine,</span>
  <span m="2980270">so</span> <span m="2980390">we're</span> <span m="2980500">going</span>
  <span m="2980630">to</span> <span m="2980690">draw</span> <span m="2980900">our</span>
  <span m="2981090">arrow</span> <span m="2981450">toward</span> <span m="2981790">the</span>
  <span m="2981860">chlorine</span> <span m="2982320">atom.</span></p><p><span m="2983290">So,</span>
  <span m="2983520">we</span> <span m="2983660">measure</span> <span m="2984040">this</span>
